<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ัะตะฝะฐั.html>ัะตะฝะฐฬั</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">senรกt</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">โ</span><span class="mention-gloss">senate</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">โ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ัะบะธะน</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-skij</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">โ</span><span class="mention-gloss">adjectival suffix</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">โ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ัะตะฝะฐััะบะธะน.html>ัะตะฝะฐฬััะบะธะน</a></strong> โข (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">senรกtskij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>senate, senatorial</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ัะตะฝั.html>ัะตะฝะธ</a> (9760)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Plural of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ัะตะฝั.html>ัะตะฝั</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">senสน</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ัะตะฝั.html>ัะตฬะฝะธ</a></strong> โข (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sรฉni</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> <abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ัะตะฝั.html>ัะตะฝะตฬะน</a></b>, <i>plural only</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>hall, vestibule, entrance hall <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a room between the porch and the habitable part of a house where people leave their boots and overcoats; especially in rustic homes</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> railroad carriage platform, tambour</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
